Question: Two numbers are said to be relatively prime if they share no common positive factors other than 1. Set S contains the set of integers from 1 to 1,000, inclusive. What is the probability that a number chosen from S is relatively prime to 1,000? # Answer option: ['A)5/7', 'B)3/5', 'C)4/7', 'D)2/5', 'E)2/7']
### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
To determine the probability that a number chosen from set S is relatively prime to 1,000, we need to focus on the definition of relatively prime numbers and the composition of set S. The key facts are the definition of relatively prime numbers and the range of integers in set S.

### Key Facts:
relatively prime if they share no common positive factors other than 1
Set S contains the set of integers from 1 to 1,000, inclusive

### Reformatted Question:
Two numbers are said to be relatively prime if they share no common positive factors other than 1. Set S contains the set of integers from 1 to 1,000, inclusive. What is the probability that a number chosen from S is relatively prime to 1,000? # Answer option: ['A)5/7', 'B)3/5', 'C)4/7', 'D)2/5', 'E)2/7']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
Two numbers are said to be relatively prime if they share no common positive factors other than 1. Set S contains the set of integers from 1 to 1,000, inclusive. What is the probability that a number chosen from S is relatively prime to 1,000? # Answer option: ['A)5/7', 'B)3/5', 'C)4/7', 'D)2/5', 'E)2/7']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine the probability that a number chosen from Set S is relatively prime to 1,000, we need to find the numbers in Set S that are relatively prime to 1,000.

Step 1: Understanding Relatively Prime
Two numbers are said to be relatively prime if they share no common positive factors other than 1.

Step 2: Set S
Set S contains the set of integers from 1 to 1,000, inclusive. This means there are 1,000 numbers in Set S.

Step 3: Prime Factorization of 1,000
The prime factorization of 1,000 is \(2^3 \times 5^3\).

Step 4: Using Euler's Totient Function
Euler's Totient Function, \(\phi(n)\), gives the count of numbers up to \(n\) that are relatively prime to \(n\). For \(n = 1,000\), the formula is:
\[
\phi(1,000) = 1,000 \times \left(1 - \frac{1}{2}\right) \times \left(1 - \frac{1}{5}\right)
\]

Step 5: Calculating \(\phi(1,000)\)
\[
\phi(1,000) = 1,000 \times \frac{1}{2} \times \frac{4}{5} = 1,000 \times \frac{4}{10} = 1,000 \times 0.4 = 400
\]

Step 6: Probability Calculation
The probability that a number chosen from Set S is relatively prime to 1,000 is the ratio of numbers that are relatively prime to 1,000 to the total numbers in Set S:
\[
\frac{\phi(1,000)}{1,000} = \frac{400}{1,000} = \frac{2}{5}
\]

Therefore, the probability that a number chosen from Set S is relatively prime to 1,000 is {D)2/5}.
Final Answer: d)2/5
Ground Truth Answer: d
Question: A point on the edge of a fan blade that is rotating in a plane 10 centimeters from the center of the fan. What is the distance traveled, in centimeters, by this point after 30 seconds when the fan runs at the rate of 300 revolutions per minutes? # Answer option: ['A)750pi', 'B)1500pi', 'C)1875pi', 'D)3000pi', 'E)7500pi']
### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
To determine the distance traveled by a point on the edge of a fan blade, we need to know the radius of the circle described by the point and the rate at which the fan is rotating. The radius is given as the distance from the center of the fan to the point, and the rate of rotation is given in revolutions per minute. These two pieces of information are essential to calculate the total distance traveled in a given time.

### Key Facts:
10 centimeters from the center of the fan
300 revolutions per minute

### Reformatted Question:
A point on the edge of a fan blade that is rotating in a plane 10 centimeters from the center of the fan. What is the distance traveled, in centimeters, by this point after 30 seconds when the fan runs at the rate of 300 revolutions per minute? # Answer option: ['A)750pi', 'B)1500pi', 'C)1875pi', 'D)3000pi', 'E)7500pi']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
A point on the edge of a fan blade that is rotating in a plane 10 centimeters from the center of the fan. What is the distance traveled, in centimeters, by this point after 30 seconds when the fan runs at the rate of 300 revolutions per minute? # Answer option: ['A)750pi', 'B)1500pi', 'C)1875pi', 'D)3000pi', 'E)7500pi']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine the distance traveled by a point on the edge of a fan blade, we need to calculate the circumference of the circle traced by the point and then determine how many times the point travels around this circle in the given time.

1. **Calculate the Circumference of the Circle:**
- The radius of the circle is given as 10 centimeters from the center of the fan.
- The formula for the circumference of a circle is \( C = 2\pi r \).
- Substituting the radius, \( C = 2\pi \times 10 = 20\pi \) centimeters.

2. **Determine the Number of Revolutions in 30 Seconds:**
- The fan runs at a rate of 300 revolutions per minute.
- In 30 seconds, which is half a minute, the fan will complete \( \frac{300}{2} = 150 \) revolutions.

3. **Calculate the Total Distance Traveled:**
- The distance traveled by the point is the number of revolutions multiplied by the circumference of the circle.
- Total distance = \( 150 \times 20\pi = 3000\pi \) centimeters.

Therefore, the distance traveled by the point on the edge of the fan blade after 30 seconds is {D)3000pi}.
Final Answer: d)3000pi

The bus fare of one adult is Rs. 140 from Ranchi to Patna and bus fare of a child is half the fare of one adult between the same places. What is the total bus fare of 4 adults and 3 children between same places? # Answer option: ['A)Rs. 666', 'B)Rs. 670', 'C)Rs. 700', 'D)Rs. 570', 'E)Rs. 770']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To find the total bus fare for 4 adults and 3 children, we need to calculate the fare for each group separately and then sum them up.

1. **Calculate the fare for adults:**
- The fare for one adult is Rs. 140.
- Therefore, the fare for 4 adults is 4 times Rs. 140.
- 4 adults x Rs. 140/adult = Rs. 560.

2. **Calculate the fare for children:**
- The fare for one child is half the fare of one adult, which is half of Rs. 140.
- Half of Rs. 140 is Rs. 70.
- Therefore, the fare for 3 children is 3 times Rs. 70.
- 3 children x Rs. 70/child = Rs. 210.

3. **Calculate the total fare:**
- Total fare = Fare for adults + Fare for children
- Total fare = Rs. 560 + Rs. 210 = Rs. 770.

Thus, the total bus fare for 4 adults and 3 children is {E)Rs. 770}.

Let A and B be independent events with P (A) = 0.2 and P(B) = 0.8. Find P(A/B)?
# Answer option: ['A)0.2', 'B)0.4', 'C)0.6', 'D)1.2', 'E)1.5']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To find \( P(A/B) \), we need to use the definition of conditional probability. For independent events, the conditional probability \( P(A/B) \) is simply \( P(A) \) because the occurrence of event B does not affect the probability of event A.

Given:
- \( P(A) = 0.2 \)
- \( P(B) = 0.8 \)

Therefore, \( P(A/B) = 0.2 \).

The correct answer is {A)0.2}.

A sporting goods store carries only yellow and white golf balls. At the beginning of the day it had 600 golf balls in stock, and by the end of the day it had sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls. If the store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, and in doing so sold all of its white golf balls, how many yellow golf balls did the store have to begin the day? # Answer option: ['A)80', 'B)120', 'C)240', 'D)320', 'E)360']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine how many yellow golf balls the store had at the beginning of the day.

1. **Total Golf Balls at the Start**: The store had 600 golf balls in stock at the beginning of the day.

2. **Golf Balls Sold**: By the end of the day, the store had sold 80% of its inventory. Therefore, the number of golf balls sold is 80% of 600, which is 0.8 * 600 = 480 golf balls.

3. **Equal Number of Yellow and White Balls Sold**: The store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls. Since it sold all of its white golf balls, the number of white golf balls sold is half of the total golf balls sold, which is 480 / 2 = 240 white golf balls.

4. **Initial Number of White Golf Balls**: Since the store sold all of its white golf balls, it initially had 240 white golf balls.

5. **Initial Number of Yellow Golf Balls**: The total number of golf balls at the start was 600. Since there were 240 white golf balls, the number of yellow golf balls at the start is 600 - 240 = 360 yellow golf balls.

Therefore, the store had {360} yellow golf balls at the beginning of the day.
Final Answer: 360
Ground Truth Answer: e

To find the greatest value for the probability that neither Stock A nor Stock B will increase in value, we need to calculate the probability that both events do not occur.

Step 1: Calculate the probability that Stock A does not increase in value.
The probability that Stock A will increase is 0.56. Therefore, the probability that Stock A does not increase is 1 - 0.56 = 0.44.

Step 2: Calculate the probability that Stock B does not increase in value.
The probability that Stock B will increase is 0.74. Therefore, the probability that Stock B does not increase is 1 - 0.74 = 0.26.

Step 3: Calculate the probability that neither Stock A nor Stock B increases in value.
Assuming the events are independent, the probability that neither event occurs is the product of their individual probabilities of not occurring:
0.44 * 0.26 = 0.1144.

The greatest value for the probability that neither of these two events will occur is 0.1144, which is not listed among the options. Therefore, we need to consider the options provided and choose the closest one, which is 'A) 0.22'.

--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine the total number of students, which is a four-digit number, and find the difference between the maximum and minimum possible numbers of students based on the given fractions.

1. **Understanding the Fractions:**
- 1/16 of the students study math
- 1/10 of the students study bio
- 1/8 of the students study english

2. **Finding a Common Denominator:**
- The least common multiple of 16, 10, and 8 is 80. This means the total number of students must be a multiple of 80.

3. **Constraints on the Total Number of Students:**
- The total number of students is a 4-digit number. Therefore, the total number of students must be between 1000 and 9999.

4. **Calculating the Range of Possible Student Numbers:**
- The smallest four-digit number that is a multiple of 80 is 1000 (since 1000 ÷ 80 = 12.5, rounded up to the nearest whole number gives 13, and 13 × 80 = 1040).
- The largest four-digit number that is a multiple of 80 is 9920 (since 9999 ÷ 80 = 124.9875, rounded down to the nearest whole number gives 124, and 124 × 80 = 9920).

5. **Calculating the Difference:**
- The difference between the maximum and minimum number of students is 9920 - 1040 = 8880.

Therefore, the difference between the maximum and minimum number of students is {A)8880}.

Question: M men agree to purchase a gift for Rs. D. If 3 men drop out how much more will each have to contribute towards the purchase of the gift? # Answer option: ['A)D/(M-3)', 'B)MD/3', 'C)M/(D-3)', 'D)3D/(M2-3M)', 'E)None of these']
### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
To determine how much more each remaining man will have to contribute if 3 men drop out, we need to focus on the initial number of men, the cost of the gift, and the change in the number of contributors. The key facts are the total number of men (M) and the cost of the gift (D). The fact that 3 men drop out is also crucial to understanding the change in the number of contributors.

### Key Facts:
M men agree to purchase a gift for Rs. D
3 men drop out

### Reformatted Question:
M men agree to purchase a gift for Rs. D. If 3 men drop out how much more will each have to contribute towards the purchase of the gift? # Answer option: ['A)D/(M-3)', 'B)MD/3', 'C)M/(D-3)', 'D)3D/(M2-3M)', 'E)None of these']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
M men agree to purchase a gift for Rs. D. If 3 men drop out how much more will each have to contribute towards the purchase of the gift? # Answer option: ['A)D/(M-3)', 'B)MD/3', 'C)M/(D-3)', 'D)3D/(M2-3M)', 'E)None of these']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine how much more each remaining man will have to contribute if 3 men drop out of the original group of M men who agreed to purchase a gift for Rs. D.

Step 1: Calculate the original contribution per man.
M men agree to purchase a gift for Rs. D. Therefore, the original contribution per man is D/M.

Step 2: Calculate the new contribution per man after 3 men drop out.
3 men drop out, so the number of remaining men is M - 3. The new contribution per man is D/(M - 3).

Step 3: Determine the additional contribution required per man.
The additional contribution required per man is the difference between the new contribution and the original contribution:
\[ \text{Additional contribution} = \frac{D}{M-3} - \frac{D}{M} \]

Step 4: Simplify the expression for the additional contribution.
\[ \text{Additional contribution} = \frac{D(M) - D(M-3)}{M(M-3)} \]
\[ = \frac{DM - D(M-3)}{M(M-3)} \]
\[ = \frac{DM - DM + 3D}{M(M-3)} \]
\[ = \frac{3D}{M(M-3)} \]

This matches none of the given options exactly, but it is closest to option D, which is \(\frac{3D}{M^2 - 3M}\).

Therefore, the correct answer is {D}.
Final Answer: d
Ground Truth Answer: d

- The cafeteria is open from Monday to Friday, which gives him 5 days to choose from for his lunches.

After flipping for twenty times none of the both won or lost any amount. How many times did the coin landed on Heads ? # Answer option: ['A)10', 'B)23', 'C)16', 'D)18', 'E)12']
### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
To determine how many times the coin landed on heads, we need to focus on the rules of the bet and the outcome. The key facts are the number of times the coin is flipped, the amount exchanged for heads and tails, and the final result of the bet where neither won nor lost any money.

coin will be flipped twenty times

### Reformatted Question:
Christopher and Jonathan were having bets. They decide that a coin will be flipped twenty times and each time it turns heads, Christopher will give $2 to Jonathan and each time it turns out to be Tails, Jonathan will give 3$ to Christopher. After flipping for twenty times none of the both won or lost any amount. How many times did the coin landed on Heads? # Answer option: ['A)10', 'B)23', 'C)16', 'D)18', 'E)12']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
Christopher and Jonathan were having bets. They decide that a coin will be flipped twenty times and each time it turns heads, Christopher will give $2 to Jonathan and each time it turns out to be Tails, Jonathan will give 3$ to Christopher. After flipping for twenty times none of the both won or lost any amount. How many times did the coin landed on Heads? # Answer option: ['A)10', 'B)23', 'C)16', 'D)18', 'E)12']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine how many times the coin landed on heads such that neither Christopher nor Jonathan won or lost any money after flipping the coin twenty times.

Let's denote:
- \( H \) as the number of times the coin landed on heads.
- \( T \) as the number of times the coin landed on tails.

From the problem, we know:
- The coin will be flipped twenty times, so \( H + T = 20 \).
- Each time it turns heads, Christopher will give $2 to Jonathan, so Jonathan earns \( 2H \) dollars from heads.
- Each time it turns out to be tails, Jonathan will give $3 to Christopher, so Christopher earns \( 3T \) dollars from tails.
- After flipping for twenty times none of the both won or lost any amount, meaning the total money exchanged is zero: \( 2H = 3T \).

We have two equations:
1. \( H + T = 20 \)
2. \( 2H = 3T \)

From the second equation, we can express \( T \) in terms of \( H \):
\[ T = \frac{2H}{3} \]

Substitute \( T = \frac{2H}{3} \) into the first equation:
\[ H + \frac{2H}{3} = 20 \]

Multiply through by 3 to eliminate the fraction:
\[ 3H + 2H = 60 \]
\[ 5H = 60 \]
\[ H = 12 \]

Thus, the coin landed on heads 12 times. Therefore, the answer is {E}.
Final Answer: e
Ground Truth Answer: e

1. **Initial Positions:**
- Neha is 12th from the left end.
- Radha is 6th from the right end.

2. **Shifting Positions:**
- Radha is shifted to the left by 2 places, so her new position is 8th from the right end.
- Neha is shifted to the right by 2 places, so her new position is 14th from the left end.

3. **Children Between Neha and Radha:**
- After the shifts, there are 6 children between Radha and Neha.

- Neha's new position: 14th from the left.
- Radha's new position: 14 + 6 + 1 = 21st from the left (since there are 6 children between them).

5. **Total Number of Children:**

Therefore, the total number of children in the row is {28}.

Question: A car is being driven, in a straight line and at a uniform speed, towards the base of a vertical tower. The top of the tower is observed from the car and, in the process, it takes 10 minutes for the angle of elevation to change from 45° to 60°. After how much more time will this car reach the base of the tower? # Answer option: ['A)5(√3 + 1)', 'B)6(√3 + √2)', 'C)7(√3 – 1)', 'D)8(√3 – 2)', 'E)None of these']
### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
To solve the problem, we need to focus on the movement of the car and the change in the angle of elevation. The key facts are the initial and final angles of elevation, the time it takes for this change, and the fact that the car is moving in a straight line at a uniform speed. These details are essential to calculate the remaining time for the car to reach the base of the tower.

### Key Facts:
angle of elevation to change from 45° to 60°
it takes 10 minutes
car is being driven, in a straight line and at a uniform speed

### Reformatted Question:
A car is being driven, in a straight line and at a uniform speed, towards the base of a vertical tower. The top of the tower is observed from the car and, in the process, it takes 10 minutes for the angle of elevation to change from 45° to 60°. After how much more time will this car reach the base of the tower? # Answer option: ['A)5(√3 + 1)', 'B)6(√3 + √2)', 'C)7(√3 – 1)', 'D)8(√3 – 2)', 'E)None of these']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
A car is being driven, in a straight line and at a uniform speed, towards the base of a vertical tower. The top of the tower is observed from the car and, in the process, it takes 10 minutes for the angle of elevation to change from 45° to 60°. After how much more time will this car reach the base of the tower? # Answer option: ['A)5(√3 + 1)', 'B)6(√3 + √2)', 'C)7(√3 – 1)', 'D)8(√3 – 2)', 'E)None of these']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to use trigonometry to understand the relationship between the car's position and the angle of elevation to the top of the tower.

1. **Understanding the Initial and Final Positions:**
- Initially, the angle of elevation is 45°. At this angle, the horizontal distance (d1) from the car to the base of the tower is equal to the height (h) of the tower because tan(45°) = 1, which implies h/d1 = 1, so d1 = h.
- After 10 minutes, the angle of elevation changes to 60°. At this angle, the horizontal distance (d2) from the car to the base of the tower is h/√3 because tan(60°) = √3, which implies h/d2 = √3, so d2 = h/√3.

2. **Calculating the Distance Covered in 10 Minutes:**
- The car covers the distance from d1 to d2 in 10 minutes. Therefore, the distance covered is d1 - d2 = h - h/√3 = h(1 - 1/√3).

3. **Calculating the Speed of the Car:**
- The speed of the car is the distance covered divided by the time taken. So, speed = [h(1 - 1/√3)] / 10.

4. **Calculating the Remaining Distance to the Base:**
- The remaining distance to the base of the tower when the angle is 60° is d2 = h/√3.

5. **Calculating the Time to Reach the Base:**
- The time taken to cover the remaining distance d2 at the same speed is given by:
Time = Remaining distance / Speed = (h/√3) / [h(1 - 1/√3) / 10] = 10 / (1 - 1/√3) * (1/√3).

6. **Simplifying the Expression:**
- Simplifying the expression for time:
Time = 10 * √3 / (1 - 1/√3) = 10 * √3 / [(√3 - 1)/√3] = 10 * √3 * √3 / (√3 - 1) = 10 * 3 / (√3 - 1) = 30 / (√3 - 1).

7. **Rationalizing the Denominator:**
- To rationalize the denominator, multiply numerator and denominator by (√3 + 1):
Time = (30 * (√3 + 1)) / ((√3 - 1) * (√3 + 1)) = (30 * (√3 + 1)) / (3 - 1) = 30 * (√3 + 1) / 2 = 15 * (√3 + 1).

8. **Matching with the Options:**
- The calculated time is 15 * (√3 + 1), which does not match any of the given options directly. Therefore, the correct answer is {E) None of these}.
Final Answer: false
Ground Truth Answer: a

If 40 grams of alloy X and 60 grams of alloy Y are melted and mixed to form alloy Z, what is the ratio of zinc and copper in the alloy Z? # Answer option: ['A)69:91', 'B)59:91', 'C)59:90', 'D)59:91', 'E)69:101']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine the ratio of zinc and copper in alloy Z, we need to calculate the amount of zinc and copper in alloys X and Y separately and then combine them.

Step 1: Calculate the amount of zinc and copper in alloy X.
- According to , alloy X is made by mixing zinc and copper in the ratio 6:9.
- The total parts in the ratio for X is 6 + 9 = 15.
- The amount of zinc in 40 grams of alloy X is (6/15) * 40 = 16 grams.
- The amount of copper in 40 grams of alloy X is (9/15) * 40 = 24 grams.

Step 2: Calculate the amount of zinc and copper in alloy Y.
- According to , alloy Y is made by mixing zinc and copper in the ratio 7:11.
- The total parts in the ratio for Y is 7 + 11 = 18.
- The amount of zinc in 60 grams of alloy Y is (7/18) * 60 = 23.33 grams.
- The amount of copper in 60 grams of alloy Y is (11/18) * 60 = 36.67 grams.

Step 3: Combine the amounts of zinc and copper from alloys X and Y to form alloy Z.
- Total zinc in alloy Z = 16 (from X) + 23.33 (from Y) = 39.33 grams.
- Total copper in alloy Z = 24 (from X) + 36.67 (from Y) = 60.67 grams.

Step 4: Calculate the ratio of zinc to copper in alloy Z.
- The ratio of zinc to copper in alloy Z is 39.33:60.67.
- To simplify, multiply both parts of the ratio by 3 to eliminate decimals: 39.33 * 3 = 118 and 60.67 * 3 = 182.
- The simplified ratio is approximately 59:91.

Therefore, the ratio of zinc to copper in alloy Z is {D)59:91}.
Final Answer: d)59:91

1. **Understanding the Variables:**
- M = abc is a three-digit number. This means M can be expressed as \(100a + 10b + c\).
- N = cba. This means N can be expressed as \(100c + 10b + a\).

2. **Given Conditions:**
- M > N. This implies \(100a + 10b + c > 100c + 10b + a\).
- Simplifying the inequality: \(99a > 99c\), which implies \(a > c\).

3. **Equation to Solve:**

\(a + 3c = 10\).

5. **Finding Possible Values:**

- \(a = 7, c = 1\)
- \(a = 8, c = 2\)
- \(a = 9, c = 3\)

7. **Counting Values of M Greater than 300:**
- All calculated values of M are greater than 300.

1. The initial cost for the first quarter-mile is $3.50.
2. After the first quarter-mile, each additional quarter-mile costs 10 cents.

Step-by-step calculation:

- First, subtract the initial cost from the total amount you have:
\[
\text{Remaining money} = \text{\$8.50} - \text{\$3.50} = \text{\$5.00}
\]

- Next, calculate how many additional quarter-miles you can afford with the remaining $5.00:
\[
\text{Number of additional quarter-miles} = \frac{\text{\$5.00}}{\text{\$0.10}} = 50 \text{ quarter-miles}
\]

\]

### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
To determine the perimeter of the original square piece of cloth, we need to understand the transformation from the square to the triangles. The key facts involve the trimming of the square to form a rectangle and the area of the resulting triangles. ### Key Facts:

area of each of triangle is 70 square feet

### Reformatted Question:
A square piece of cloth is trimmed by 4 feet on one edge to form a rectangular piece, which is then cut diagonally in half to create two triangles. If the area of each of triangle is 70 square feet, what was the perimeter (in feet) of the original piece of square cloth? # Answer option: ['A)56', 'B)58', 'C)60', 'D)62', 'E)64']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
A square piece of cloth is trimmed by 4 feet on one edge to form a rectangular piece, which is then cut diagonally in half to create two triangles. If the area of each of triangle is 70 square feet, what was the perimeter (in feet) of the original piece of square cloth? # Answer option: ['A)56', 'B)58', 'C)60', 'D)62', 'E)64']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine the side length of the original square piece of cloth and then calculate its perimeter.

Step 1: Understand the problem setup
- We start with a square piece of cloth.
- One edge of the square is trimmed by 4 feet to form a rectangle.
- This rectangle is then cut diagonally to form two right triangles.

Step 2: Use the area of the triangles
- The area of each triangle is given as 70 square feet.
- Since the rectangle is cut diagonally, the two triangles are congruent, and the area of the rectangle is twice the area of one triangle, which is 2 * 70 = 140 square feet.

Step 3: Determine the dimensions of the rectangle
- Let the original side length of the square be \( s \).
- After trimming 4 feet from one edge, the dimensions of the rectangle are \( s \) and \( s - 4 \).
- The area of the rectangle is \( s \times (s - 4) = 140 \).

Step 4: Solve for \( s \)
- We have the equation: \( s \times (s - 4) = 140 \).
- Expanding this gives: \( s^2 - 4s = 140 \).
- Rearranging gives: \( s^2 - 4s - 140 = 0 \).

Step 5: Solve the quadratic equation
- Using the quadratic formula \( s = \frac{-b \pm \sqrt{b^2 - 4ac}}{2a} \), where \( a = 1 \), \( b = -4 \), and \( c = -140 \):
- The discriminant is \( b^2 - 4ac = (-4)^2 - 4 \times 1 \times (-140) = 16 + 560 = 576 \).
- The square root of 576 is 24.
- So, \( s = \frac{4 \pm 24}{2} \).

Step 6: Calculate the possible values for \( s \)
- \( s = \frac{4 + 24}{2} = 14 \) (since side lengths must be positive, we discard the negative solution).

Step 7: Calculate the perimeter of the original square
- The original side length of the square is \( s = 14 \).
- The perimeter of the square is \( 4 \times 14 = 56 \).

Therefore, the perimeter of the original piece of square cloth is {56}.
Final Answer: 56
Ground Truth Answer: a

walk 10 steps and stop, you reach to the ground in 20 minutes

### Reformatted Question:
Consider there is an staircase elevator and you are coming down. If you walk 20 steps and stop, then you reach bottom in 10 minutes. If you walk 10 steps and stop, you reach to the ground in 20 minutes. What is the speed of the elevator? # Answer option: ['A)1 step/minute', 'B)2 step/minute', 'C)3 step/minute', 'D)4 step/minute', 'E)None of the above']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
Consider there is an staircase elevator and you are coming down. If you walk 20 steps and stop, then you reach bottom in 10 minutes. If you walk 10 steps and stop, you reach to the ground in 20 minutes. What is the speed of the elevator? # Answer option: ['A)1 step/minute', 'B)2 step/minute', 'C)3 step/minute', 'D)4 step/minute', 'E)None of the above']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine the speed of the elevator, we need to analyze the information given in the facts:

1. When you walk 20 steps and stop, you reach the bottom in 10 minutes.
2. When you walk 10 steps and stop, you reach the ground in 20 minutes.

Let's denote the total number of steps from the top to the bottom as \( S \), and the speed of the elevator as \( v \) steps per minute.

From , if you walk 20 steps and then stop, the elevator takes you the rest of the way in 10 minutes. This means the elevator covers \( S - 20 \) steps in 10 minutes. Therefore, the equation is:
\[ S - 20 = 10v \]

From , if you walk 10 steps and then stop, the elevator takes you the rest of the way in 20 minutes. This means the elevator covers \( S - 10 \) steps in 20 minutes. Therefore, the equation is:
\[ S - 10 = 20v \]

Now, we have two equations:
1. \( S - 20 = 10v \)
2. \( S - 10 = 20v \)

We can solve these equations simultaneously. Subtract the first equation from the second:
\[ (S - 10) - (S - 20) = 20v - 10v \]
\[ 10 = 10v \]
\[ v = 1 \]

Thus, the speed of the elevator is 1 step per minute. Therefore, the answer is {A)1 step/minute}.
Final Answer: a)1 step/minute
Ground Truth Answer: a

To determine the interest rate, we need to calculate the total amount paid back and compare it to the original amount borrowed.

1. **Calculate the total amount paid back:**
- The man pays back in 12 monthly installments of Rs.31.50.
- Total amount paid back = 12 * 31.50 = Rs.378.

2. **Determine the interest paid:**
- The original amount borrowed is Rs.360.
- Interest paid = Total amount paid back - Original amount borrowed = 378 - 360 = Rs.18.

3. **Calculate the interest rate:**
- The interest rate is calculated on the original amount borrowed.
- Interest rate = (Interest paid / Original amount borrowed) * 100 = (18 / 360) * 100 = 5%.

Therefore, the interest rate is {D)5%}.

--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
A hollow cube of size 5cm is taken, with the thickness of 1cm. It is made of smaller cubes of size 1cm. If the outer surface of the cube is painted, how many faces of the smaller cubes remain unpainted? # Answer option: ['A)438', 'B)550', 'C)500', 'D)450', 'E)498']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine how many faces of the smaller cubes remain unpainted when the outer surface of a hollow cube is painted.

1. **Understanding the Structure**:
- We have a hollow cube of size 5cm.
- The cube is 1cm thick.
- It is made of smaller cubes of size 1cm.

2. **Calculating the Total Number of Smaller Cubes**:
- The outer cube is 5cm on each side, so it contains \(5 \times 5 \times 5 = 125\) smaller cubes.

3. **Calculating the Inner Hollow Part**:
- The hollow part is a cube of size \(5 - 2 \times 1 = 3cm\) (since the thickness is 1cm on each side).
- The inner hollow cube contains \(3 \times 3 \times 3 = 27\) smaller cubes.

4. **Calculating the Number of Smaller Cubes in the Shell**:
- The shell of the hollow cube is the total number of smaller cubes minus the inner hollow part: \(125 - 27 = 98\) smaller cubes.

5. **Painting the Outer Surface**:
- When the outer surface of the cube is painted, each face of the outer shell cubes that is exposed will be painted.

6. **Calculating Unpainted Faces**:
- Each smaller cube has 6 faces.
- The total number of faces for all 98 smaller cubes is \(98 \times 6 = 588\) faces.
- The outer surface of the 5cm cube has \(5 \times 5 \times 6 = 150\) faces painted (since each face of the cube is 5x5 and there are 6 faces).
- Therefore, the number of unpainted faces is \(588 - 150 = 438\).

Thus, the number of faces of the smaller cubes that remain unpainted is {438}.
Final Answer: 438

While selling a watch, a shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%. If he gives a discount of 7%, he earns Rs. 15 less as profit. The marked price of the watch is:
# Answer option: ['A)Rs. 697.50', 'B)Rs. 712.50', 'C)Rs. 787.50', 'D)Rs. 750', 'E)Rs. 780']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine the marked price of the watch using the given information about discounts and profit.

1. Let's denote the marked price of the watch as \( M \).

2. When the shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%, the selling price is \( 0.95M \).

3. When the shopkeeper gives a discount of 7%, the selling price is \( 0.93M \).

4. According to he earns Rs. 15 less as profit when giving a 7% discount compared to a 5% discount. This means the difference in selling prices is Rs. 15.

5. Therefore, we can set up the equation:
\[
0.95M - 0.93M = 15
\]

6. Simplifying the equation gives:
\[
0.02M = 15
\]

7. Solving for \( M \), we divide both sides by 0.02:
\[

\]

Thus, the marked price of the watch is Rs. 750. The correct answer is {D}.

If 36 ≤ n ≤ 72, then x = (n^2 + 2√n(n + 4) + 16) / (n + 4√n + 4) satisfies
# Answer option: ['A)20 < x < 54', 'B)23 < x < 58', 'C)25 < x < 64', 'D)28 < x < 60', 'E)None of these']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to analyze the expression for \( x \) given by the equation:

\( x = \frac{n^2 + 2\sqrt{n}(n + 4) + 16}{n + 4\sqrt{n} + 4} \)

and determine the range of \( x \) for the given range of \( n \):

\( 36 \leq n \leq 72 \).

Let's break down the expression for \( x \):

1. **Numerator Analysis**:
- The numerator is \( n^2 + 2\sqrt{n}(n + 4) + 16 \).
- This can be expanded to \( n^2 + 2n\sqrt{n} + 8\sqrt{n} + 16 \).

2. **Denominator Analysis**:
- The denominator is \( n + 4\sqrt{n} + 4 \).

3. **Behavior of the Expression**:
- As \( n \) increases from 36 to 72, both the numerator and the denominator increase.
- The expression is a rational function, and we need to determine how it behaves over the interval.

4. **Boundary Values**:
- Calculate \( x \) at the boundary values of \( n \) to estimate the range of \( x \).

5. **Substitute \( n = 36 \) and \( n = 72 \) into the expression**:
- For \( n = 36 \):
- Numerator: \( 36^2 + 2\sqrt{36}(36 + 4) + 16 = 1296 + 2 \times 6 \times 40 + 16 = 1296 + 480 + 16 = 1792 \).
- Denominator: \( 36 + 4 \times 6 + 4 = 36 + 24 + 4 = 64 \).
- \( x = \frac{1792}{64} = 28 \).

- For \( n = 72 \):
- Numerator: \( 72^2 + 2\sqrt{72}(72 + 4) + 16 = 5184 + 2 \times 8.485 \times 76 + 16 \).
- Approximate \( \sqrt{72} \approx 8.485 \).
- Numerator: \( 5184 + 2 \times 8.485 \times 76 + 16 \approx 5184 + 1288.36 + 16 = 6488.36 \).
- Denominator: \( 72 + 4 \times 8.485 + 4 = 72 + 33.94 + 4 = 109.94 \).
- \( x \approx \frac{6488.36}{109.94} \approx 59 \).

6. **Range of \( x \)**:
- From the calculations, \( x \) ranges from approximately 28 to 59 as \( n \) varies from 36 to 72.

7. **Conclusion**:
- The range of \( x \) is \( 28 < x < 60 \).

Therefore, the correct answer is {D}.
Final Answer: d

Question: The sum of the digits of a three digit number is 17, and the sum of the squares of its digits is 109. If we subtract 495 from the number, we shall get a number consisting of the same digits written in the reverse order. Find the number. # Answer option: ['A)368', 'B)377', 'C)288', 'D)997', 'E)112']
### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
To solve this problem, we need to identify the conditions that the three-digit number must satisfy. The key facts are the sum of the digits, the sum of the squares of the digits, and the condition involving reversing the digits after subtracting 495. These conditions are essential to determine the correct number from the given options.

### Key Facts:
The sum of the digits of a three digit number is 17
the sum of the squares of its digits is 109
If we subtract 495 from the number, we shall get a number consisting of the same digits written in the reverse order

### Reformatted Question:
The sum of the digits of a three digit number is 17, and the sum of the squares of its digits is 109. If we subtract 495 from the number, we shall get a number consisting of the same digits written in the reverse order. Find the number. # Answer option: ['A)368', 'B)377', 'C)288', 'D)997', 'E)112']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
The sum of the digits of a three digit number is 17, and the sum of the squares of its digits is 109. If we subtract 495 from the number, we shall get a number consisting of the same digits written in the reverse order. Find the number. # Answer option: ['A)368', 'B)377', 'C)288', 'D)997', 'E)112']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to find a three-digit number that satisfies all the given conditions. Let's denote the three-digit number as \( \overline{abc} \), where \( a \), \( b \), and \( c \) are the digits of the number.

Step 1: Use the sum of the digits.
According to , the sum of the digits is 17:
\[ a + b + c = 17 \]

Step 2: Use the sum of the squares of the digits.
According to , the sum of the squares of the digits is 109:
\[ a^2 + b^2 + c^2 = 109 \]

Step 3: Use the condition about reversing the digits.
According to , subtracting 495 from the number gives the number with its digits reversed:
\[ 100a + 10b + c - 495 = 100c + 10b + a \]

Simplifying this equation:
\[ 100a + 10b + c - 495 = 100c + 10b + a \]
\[ 99a - 99c = 495 \]
\[ a - c = 5 \]

Step 4: Solve the system of equations.
We have three equations:
1. \( a + b + c = 17 \)
2. \( a^2 + b^2 + c^2 = 109 \)
3. \( a - c = 5 \)

From equation 3, we have:
\[ a = c + 5 \]

Substitute \( a = c + 5 \) into equation 1:
\[ (c + 5) + b + c = 17 \]
\[ 2c + b = 12 \]
\[ b = 12 - 2c \]

Substitute \( a = c + 5 \) and \( b = 12 - 2c \) into equation 2:
\[ (c + 5)^2 + (12 - 2c)^2 + c^2 = 109 \]

Expanding and simplifying:
\[ (c^2 + 10c + 25) + (144 - 48c + 4c^2) + c^2 = 109 \]
\[ 6c^2 - 38c + 169 = 109 \]
\[ 6c^2 - 38c + 60 = 0 \]

Divide the entire equation by 2:
\[ 3c^2 - 19c + 30 = 0 \]

Solve this quadratic equation using the quadratic formula:
\[ c = \frac{-b \pm \sqrt{b^2 - 4ac}}{2a} \]
where \( a = 3 \), \( b = -19 \), and \( c = 30 \).

\[ c = \frac{19 \pm \sqrt{(-19)^2 - 4 \cdot 3 \cdot 30}}{6} \]
\[ c = \frac{19 \pm \sqrt{361 - 360}}{6} \]
\[ c = \frac{19 \pm 1}{6} \]

This gives us two possible values for \( c \):
\[ c = \frac{20}{6} = \frac{10}{3} \] (not an integer, discard)
\[ c = \frac{18}{6} = 3 \]

So, \( c = 3 \).

Substitute \( c = 3 \) back into \( a = c + 5 \):
\[ a = 3 + 5 = 8 \]

Substitute \( c = 3 \) into \( b = 12 - 2c \):
\[ b = 12 - 2 \times 3 = 6 \]

Thus, the number is 368.

Verify:
- Sum of digits: \( 3 + 6 + 8 = 17 \) (correct)
- Sum of squares: \( 3^2 + 6^2 + 8^2 = 9 + 36 + 64 = 109 \) (correct)
- Reverse condition: \( 368 - 495 = -127 \), reverse of 368 is 863, and \( 863 - 368 = 495 \) (correct)

Therefore, the number is {368}.
Final Answer: 368
Ground Truth Answer: a

Question: At the of his one-year investment, Charles received $54,080, including interest and principal from a certain investment. If the investment paid an annual interest of 8 percent compounded semi-annually, which of the following is the amount of money that Charles originally invested? # Answer option: ['A)$45,000', 'B)$50,000', 'C)$54,000', 'D)$59,000', 'E)$62,000']
### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
To determine the amount of money Charles originally invested, we need to focus on the total amount he received at the end of the investment period and the interest rate details. The key facts are the total amount received, the annual interest rate, and the compounding frequency. These details are essential to calculate the original investment amount.

### Key Facts:
Charles received $54,080
annual interest of 8 percent
compounded semi-annually

### Reformatted Question:
At the end of his one-year investment, Charles received $54,080, including interest and principal from a certain investment. If the investment paid an annual interest of 8 percent compounded semi-annually, which of the following is the amount of money that Charles originally invested? # Answer option: ['A)$45,000', 'B)$50,000', 'C)$54,000', 'D)$59,000', 'E)$62,000']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
At the end of his one-year investment, Charles received $54,080, including interest and principal from a certain investment. If the investment paid an annual interest of 8 percent compounded semi-annually, which of the following is the amount of money that Charles originally invested? # Answer option: ['A)$45,000', 'B)$50,000', 'C)$54,000', 'D)$59,000', 'E)$62,000']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine the amount of money Charles originally invested, we need to use the formula for compound interest. The formula for compound interest is:

\[ A = P \left(1 + \frac{r}{n}\right)^{nt} \]

where:
- \( A \) is the amount of money accumulated after n years, including interest.
- \( P \) is the principal amount (the initial amount of money).
- \( r \) is the annual interest rate (decimal).
- \( n \) is the number of times that interest is compounded per year.
- \( t \) is the time the money is invested for in years.

Given:
- \( A = \) $54,080
- \( r = \) 8 percent = 0.08
- \( n = \) compounded semi-annually = 2
- \( t = 1 \) year

We need to find \( P \).

Plugging the values into the formula:

\[ 54,080 = P \left(1 + \frac{0.08}{2}\right)^{2 \times 1} \]

\[ 54,080 = P \left(1 + 0.04\right)^{2} \]

\[ 54,080 = P \left(1.04\right)^{2} \]

\[ 54,080 = P \times 1.0816 \]

To find \( P \), divide both sides by 1.0816:

\[ P = \frac{54,080}{1.0816} \]

\[ P \approx 50,000 \]

Therefore, the amount of money that Charles originally invested is approximately $50,000. The correct answer is {B}.
Final Answer: b
Ground Truth Answer: b

### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
To determine the length of the fence, we need to consider both the width of each picket and the space between them. The key facts are the width of each picket and the space between each pair of pickets. These details are essential to calculate the total length of the fence.

### Key Facts:
x pickets
1/2 inch wide
6 inches of space between each pair of pickets

### Reformatted Question:
A straight picket fence is composed of x pickets each of which is 1/2 inch wide. If there are 6 inches of space between each pair of pickets, which of the following represents the length of fence in feet?
# Answer option: ['A)13x/2', 'B)13x/2 - 6', 'C)13x/24', 'D)(13x+1)/24', 'E)(13x-12)/24']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
A straight picket fence is composed of x pickets each of which is 1/2 inch wide. If there are 6 inches of space between each pair of pickets, which of the following represents the length of fence in feet?
# Answer option: ['A)13x/2', 'B)13x/2 - 6', 'C)13x/24', 'D)(13x+1)/24', 'E)(13x-12)/24']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine the length of the fence in feet, we need to consider both the width of the pickets and the spaces between them.

1. **Width of the Pickets:**
- There are x pickets, and each picket is 1/2 inch wide.
- Therefore, the total width of the pickets is \( x \times \frac{1}{2} = \frac{x}{2} \) inches.

2. **Spaces Between the Pickets:**
- There are x pickets, which means there are \( x - 1 \) spaces between them.
- Each space is 6 inches wide.
- Therefore, the total width of the spaces is \( (x - 1) \times 6 = 6x - 6 \) inches.

3. **Total Length of the Fence:**
- The total length of the fence in inches is the sum of the width of the pickets and the width of the spaces:
\[
\frac{x}{2} + 6x - 6
\]
- Simplifying this expression:
\[
\frac{x}{2} + 6x - 6 = \frac{x}{2} + \frac{12x}{2} - \frac{12}{2} = \frac{13x - 12}{2} \text{ inches}
\]

4. **Convert Inches to Feet:**
- Since there are 12 inches in a foot, we convert the total length from inches to feet by dividing by 12:
\[
\frac{13x - 12}{2} \div 12 = \frac{13x - 12}{24} \text{ feet}
\]

Thus, the length of the fence in feet is represented by the expression \(\frac{13x - 12}{24}\).

The correct answer is {E}.
Final Answer: e
Ground Truth Answer: e

3. First, we need to determine how many 1/4 inch segments are in 20 inches. Since 1 inch is equal to 4 segments of 1/4 inch, 20 inches will have 20 * 4 = 80 segments of 1/4 inch.

- Required speed = 120 km/hr.
- Speed gain = Required speed - Initial speed = 120 km/hr - 60 km/hr = 60 km/hr.

### Fact Extraction Reasoning:

### Key Facts:

### Reformatted Question:
A merchant receives an invoice for a motor boat for $20 000 with terms 4/30, n/100. What is the highest simple interest rate at which he can afford to borrow money in order to take advantage of the discount? # Answer option: ['A)247.67', 'B)237.67', 'C)227.67', 'D)215.67', 'E)None of these']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
A merchant receives an invoice for a motor boat for $20 000 with terms 4/30, n/100. What is the highest simple interest rate at which he can afford to borrow money in order to take advantage of the discount? # Answer option: ['A)247.67', 'B)237.67', 'C)227.67', 'D)215.67', 'E)None of these']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine the highest simple interest rate at which the merchant can afford to borrow money to take advantage of the discount, we need to analyze the terms of the invoice and calculate the potential savings from the discount.

1. **Understanding the Invoice Terms:**
- The invoice amount is $20,000.
- The terms are 4/30, n/100, which means a 4% discount is available if the invoice is paid within 30 days, otherwise, the full amount is due in 100 days.

2. **Calculating the Discount:**
- A 4% discount on $20,000 is calculated as follows:
\[
\text{Discount} = 0.04 \times 20,000 = 800
\]
- Therefore, if the merchant pays within 30 days, they only need to pay:
\[
20,000 - 800 = 19,200
\]

3. **Interest Calculation:**
- The merchant can save $800 by paying early. To determine the highest interest rate they can afford, we need to calculate the interest on $19,200 for the remaining 70 days (100 - 30 days).

4. **Simple Interest Formula:**
- The simple interest formula is:
\[
\text{Interest} = \text{Principal} \times \text{Rate} \times \text{Time}
\]
- Here, the principal is $19,200, the time is 70/365 years, and the interest should not exceed the $800 savings.

5. **Setting Up the Equation:**
- We set up the equation to find the rate:
\[
800 = 19,200 \times \text{Rate} \times \frac{70}{365}
\]
- Solving for the rate:
\[
\text{Rate} = \frac{800 \times 365}{19,200 \times 70}
\]

6. **Calculating the Rate:**
- Performing the calculation:
\[
\text{Rate} = \frac{800 \times 365}{19,200 \times 70} \approx 0.21567
\]
- Converting to a percentage:
\[
\text{Rate} \approx 21.567\%
\]

7. **Conclusion:**
- The highest simple interest rate at which the merchant can afford to borrow money is approximately 21.567%. Therefore, the closest answer option is {D)215.67}.

The answer is {D}.
Final Answer: d
Ground Truth Answer: a

--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine the weight of a coin made of pure aluminum, given the properties of an alloy coin and the relative densities of aluminum and silver.

Step 1: Understand the composition of the alloy coin.
- The coin made of alloy of aluminum and silver measures 2 x 15 mm.
- The weight of the coin is 30 grams.
- The volume of aluminum in the alloy equals that of silver.

Step 2: Determine the weight contribution of each metal in the alloy coin.
- Since the volume of aluminum equals the volume of silver, and silver is twice as heavy as aluminum, the weight of silver in the coin is twice the weight of aluminum.
- Let the weight of aluminum be x grams. Then the weight of silver is 2x grams.
- The total weight of the coin is x + 2x = 3x = 30 grams.
- Solving for x gives x = 30/3 = 10 grams.

Step 3: Calculate the weight of a pure aluminum coin.
- The volume of the original alloy coin is proportional to its dimensions: 2 mm thickness and 15 mm diameter.
- The new coin is made of pure aluminum and measures 1 x 30 mm.
- The volume of the new coin is proportional to its dimensions: 1 mm thickness and 30 mm diameter.
- The volume ratio of the new coin to the original coin is (1 x 30) / (2 x 15) = 1.
- Since the volume ratio is 1, the weight of the new pure aluminum coin is the same as the weight of aluminum in the original coin, which is 10 grams.

However, the problem asks for the weight of a coin made of pure aluminum, and we need to consider the volume change:
- The new coin has a volume ratio of (1 x 30) / (2 x 15) = 1, meaning it has the same volume as the aluminum part of the original coin.
- Therefore, the weight of the new pure aluminum coin is 10 grams.

The answer is {A)36 grams}.
Final Answer: a)36 grams

If x<0, y>0, and |x^3| > |y^2|, which of the following must be true?
# Answer option: ['A)x > y', 'B)y^2 > x^2', 'C)-x^3 < y^2', 'D)–x < y', 'E)x < –y']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to analyze the given conditions and determine which statement must be true.

1. We know that x<0. This means x is a negative number.

2. We also know that y>0. This means y is a positive number.

3. The condition |x^3| > |y^2| tells us that the absolute value of x cubed is greater than the absolute value of y squared.

Let's analyze each option:

- Option A: x > y
- Since x is negative (x<0) and y is positive (y>0), x cannot be greater than y. Therefore, this option is false.

- Option B: y^2 > x^2
- Since y is positive, y^2 is also positive. However, x is negative, and x^2 is positive. The condition |x^3| > |y^2| does not directly imply y^2 > x^2. Therefore, this option is not necessarily true.

- Option C: -x^3 < y^2
- Since x is negative, x^3 is also negative, and -x^3 is positive. Given |x^3| > |y^2|, it implies that -x^3 (which is positive) is greater than y^2. Therefore, this option is false.

- Option D: –x < y
- Since x is negative, -x is positive. Given |x^3| > |y^2|, it implies that the magnitude of x is larger than the magnitude of y. Therefore, -x (positive) is greater than y (positive). This option is true.

- Option E: x < –y
- Since x is negative and y is positive, -y is negative. Therefore, x cannot be less than -y. This option is false.

Based on the analysis, the statement that must be true is option D: –x < y.

The answer is {D}.
Final Answer: d
Ground Truth Answer: b

### Reformatted Question:

--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
Janice bikes at 10 miles per hour, while Jennie bikes at 20. How long until they have collectively biked 1 mile? # Answer option: ['A)1 minute', 'B)2 minutes', 'C)3 minutes', 'D)4 minutes', 'E)5 minutes']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine how long it will take for Janice and Jennie to collectively bike 1 mile, we need to calculate their combined biking rate and then find the time required to cover 1 mile at that rate.

1. **Calculate Janice's biking rate in miles per minute:**
- Janice bikes at 10 miles per hour.
- To convert this to miles per minute, divide by 60 (since there are 60 minutes in an hour):
\[
\frac{10 \text{ miles per hour}}{60 \text{ minutes per hour}} = \frac{1}{6} \text{ miles per minute}
\]

2. **Calculate Jennie's biking rate in miles per minute:**
- Jennie bikes at 20 miles per hour.
- Similarly, convert this to miles per minute:
\[
\frac{20 \text{ miles per hour}}{60 \text{ minutes per hour}} = \frac{1}{3} \text{ miles per minute}
\]

3. **Calculate their combined biking rate:**
- Add Janice's and Jennie's rates together:
\[
\frac{1}{6} + \frac{1}{3} = \frac{1}{6} + \frac{2}{6} = \frac{3}{6} = \frac{1}{2} \text{ miles per minute}
\]

4. **Determine the time to bike 1 mile collectively:**
- Since they bike at a combined rate of \(\frac{1}{2}\) mile per minute, it will take them:
\[
\frac{1 \text{ mile}}{\frac{1}{2} \text{ miles per minute}} = 2 \text{ minutes}
\]

Therefore, the time it will take for Janice and Jennie to collectively bike 1 mile is {B)2 minutes}.

Question: A father wants to divide Rs. 5100 between his two sons, Mohan and Sohan who are 23 and 24 at present. ### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
To determine Mohan's share, we need to focus on the total amount to be divided, the ages of Mohan and Sohan, and the condition that their shares will grow to equal amounts by the time they are both 26 years old, given a compound interest rate. These details are essential to set up the equations needed to solve the problem.

### Key Facts:
Rs. 5100
Mohan and Sohan who are 23 and 24 at present
compound interest at 4% p.a.
equal amount on attaining the age of 26 years

### Reformatted Question:
A father wants to divide Rs. 5100 between his two sons, Mohan and Sohan who are 23 and 24 at present. He divides the amount in such a way that if their shares are invested at compound interest at 4% p.a. they will receive equal amount on attaining the age of 26 years. --------------- End of Conversation ---------------
A father wants to divide Rs. 5100 between his two sons, Mohan and Sohan who are 23 and 24 at present. He divides the amount in such a way that if their shares are invested at compound interest at 4% p.a. they will receive equal amount on attaining the age of 26 years. Find Mohan's share. # Answer option: ['A)2400', 'B)2500', 'C)2600', 'D)2700', 'E)None of these']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine how much of the Rs. 5100 should be allocated to Mohan so that both Mohan and Sohan receive the same amount when they reach the age of 26, given that their investments grow at a compound interest rate of 4% per annum.

1. **Understanding the Time Frame**:
- Mohan is currently 23 years old, so he will reach 26 in 3 years.
- Sohan is currently 24 years old, so he will reach 26 in 2 years.

2. **Compound Interest Formula**:
The formula for compound interest is:
\[
A = P \left(1 + \frac{r}{100}\right)^n
\]
where \(A\) is the amount after \(n\) years, \(P\) is the principal amount, \(r\) is the rate of interest, and \(n\) is the number of years.

3. **Setting Up the Equations**:
- Let Mohan's share be \(M\) and Sohan's share be \(S\).
- According to the problem, \(M + S = \text{Rs. } 5100\). Rs. 5100
- For Mohan, the amount after 3 years is:
\[
M \left(1 + \frac{4}{100}\right)^3 = M \times 1.124864
\]
- For Sohan, the amount after 2 years is:
\[
S \left(1 + \frac{4}{100}\right)^2 = S \times 1.0816
\]
- We need these amounts to be equal at the age of 26:
\[
M \times 1.124864 = S \times 1.0816
\]

4. **Solving the Equations**:
- From the equation \(M \times 1.124864 = S \times 1.0816\), we can express \(S\) in terms of \(M\):
\[
S = \frac{M \times 1.124864}{1.0816}
\]
- Substitute \(S\) in the total amount equation:
\[
M + \frac{M \times 1.124864}{1.0816} = 5100
\]
- Simplify and solve for \(M\):
\[
M \left(1 + \frac{1.124864}{1.0816}\right) = 5100
\]
\[
M \left(1 + 1.039999) = 5100
\]
\[
M \times 2.039999 = 5100
\]
\[
M = \frac{5100}{2.039999} \approx 2500
\]

Therefore, Mohan's share is approximately Rs. 2500. The correct answer is {B)2500}.
Final Answer: b)2500
Ground Truth Answer: b

### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
To determine how long it will take both friends to empty the jar of candies when eating together, we need to know the individual rates at which each friend can eat the candies. ### Key Facts:
P eaten alone, it would have taken him 10 minutes to finish the candies in the jar
Q eaten alone, it would have taken her 5 minutes to finish half the jar

### Reformatted Question:

Had Q eaten alone, it would have taken her 5 minutes to finish half the jar. Two friends are eating a jar full of candies. Had P eaten alone, it would have taken him 10 minutes to finish the candies in the jar. Had Q eaten alone, it would have taken her 5 minutes to finish half the jar. --------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine the combined rate at which P and Q can eat the candies and then calculate the time it would take them to finish the jar together.

Step 1: Determine P's rate of eating.
Had P eaten alone, it would have taken him 10 minutes to finish the candies in the jar. This means P's rate is 1 jar per 10 minutes, or 1/10 of the jar per minute.

Step 2: Determine Q's rate of eating.
Had Q eaten alone, it would have taken her 5 minutes to finish half the jar. This means Q's rate is 1/2 jar per 5 minutes, or 1/10 of the jar per minute.

Step 3: Calculate the combined rate of P and Q.
Since both P and Q eat at a rate of 1/10 of the jar per minute, their combined rate is:
1/10 (P's rate) + 1/10 (Q's rate) = 2/10 = 1/5 of the jar per minute.

Step 4: Calculate the time it takes for both to finish the jar together.
Since their combined rate is 1/5 of the jar per minute, it will take them 5 minutes to finish the entire jar (since 1 jar / (1/5 jar per minute) = 5 minutes).

Therefore, the answer is {B)5}.

To determine the average cost per year of the new tires and compare it to the cost of repairing the current tires, we need to calculate both costs and then find the percentage difference.

Step 1: Calculate the average cost per year of the new tires.
- The new tires last for four years.
- The cost of new tires is $180 per tire.
- Therefore, the average cost per year for new tires is $180 / 4 = $45.

Step 2: Calculate the average cost per year of repairing the current tires.
- Repairing the current tires costs $40 per tire.
- A repair makes the tires last for one additional year.
- Therefore, the average cost per year for repairing the tires is $40.

Step 3: Calculate the percentage increase from the cost of repairing to the cost of new tires.
- The difference in cost per year is $45 (new tires) - $40 (repair) = $5.
- The percentage increase is ($5 / $40) * 100% = 12.5%.

Therefore, the average cost per year of the new tires is 12.5% greater than the cost of repairing the current tires. The answer is {C}.

To determine how many times the revenue from the sale of novels was compared to the revenue from the sale of biographies, we need to analyze the given facts step by step.

1. **Calculate the revenue from novels:**
- According to , 34 percent of Ace Book Company's sales revenue came from the sale of novels. This means that if the total revenue is represented as 100%, then the revenue from novels is 34%.

2. **Calculate the remaining revenue:**
- Since 34% of the revenue is from novels, the remaining revenue is 100% - 34% = 66%.

3. **Calculate the revenue from biographies:**
- According to , 1/3 of the remaining revenue was from the sale of biographies. Therefore, the revenue from biographies is 1/3 of 66%, which is 66% / 3 = 22%.

4. **Determine how many times the revenue from novels is compared to biographies:**
- The revenue from novels is 34%, and the revenue from biographies is 22%.
- To find how many times the revenue from novels is compared to biographies, we divide the percentage of revenue from novels by the percentage of revenue from biographies: 34% / 22% = 1.545.

5. **Select the closest answer option:**
- The closest option to 1.545 is 1.5.

Therefore, the company's revenue from the sale of novels was approximately 1.5 times its revenue from the sale of biographies. The answer is {B}.

To determine the distance that ant A travels until meeting ant B, we need to calculate the time it takes for them to meet and then use that time to find the distance ant A travels.

1. **Calculate the combined speed of the ants:**
- Ant A is moving at a speed of 9 cm per hour.
- Ant B is moving at a speed of 6 cm per hour.
- Combined speed = 9 cm/hour + 6 cm/hour = 15 cm/hour.

2. **Calculate the time it takes for the ants to meet:**
- The farms are 75 cm away from each other.
- Time = Distance / Combined Speed = 75 cm / 15 cm/hour = 5 hours.

3. **Calculate the distance ant A travels:**
- Distance traveled by ant A = Speed of ant A * Time = 9 cm/hour * 5 hours = 45 cm.

Therefore, the distance that ant A travels until meeting ant B is 45 cm. The answer is {A)45}.

--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
At a conference, one team is made up of 4 men and 4 women. Four presenters are chosen to present the team's findings in front of the entire conference. How many different groups of presenters can be chosen from the team if a team cannot be composed of men only or women only? (Two groups of presenters are considered different if at least one presenter is different.)
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine the number of ways to choose 4 presenters from a team of 4 men and 4 women, with the condition that the group cannot be composed of only men or only women.

Step 1: Calculate the total number of ways to choose 4 presenters from 8 people (4 men and 4 women).
- The total number of ways to choose 4 presenters from 8 people is given by the combination formula C(n, k) = n! / (k!(n-k)!), where n is the total number of people to choose from, and k is the number of people to choose.
- So, C(8, 4) = 8! / (4! * (8-4)!) = 70.

Step 2: Calculate the number of ways to choose 4 men only.
- Since there are 4 men, the number of ways to choose 4 men is C(4, 4) = 1.

Step 3: Calculate the number of ways to choose 4 women only.
- Since there are 4 women, the number of ways to choose 4 women is C(4, 4) = 1.

Step 4: Subtract the all-men and all-women groups from the total.
- Since we cannot have a group composed of only men or only women, we subtract these cases from the total number of combinations.
- Therefore, the number of valid groups is 70 (total ways) - 1 (all men) - 1 (all women) = 68.

Thus, the number of different groups of presenters that can be chosen, ensuring that the group is not composed of only men or only women, is 68.

However, it seems there is a discrepancy with the provided answer options. Let's re-evaluate the possible combinations:

- We can have 3 men and 1 woman, 2 men and 2 women, or 1 man and 3 women.

1. Number of ways to choose 3 men and 1 woman:
- C(4, 3) for men = 4
- C(4, 1) for women = 4
- Total = 4 * 4 = 16

2. Number of ways to choose 2 men and 2 women:
- C(4, 2) for men = 6
- C(4, 2) for women = 6
- Total = 6 * 6 = 36

3. Number of ways to choose 1 man and 3 women:
- C(4, 1) for men = 4
- C(4, 3) for women = 4
- Total = 4 * 4 = 16

Adding these up gives us 16 + 36 + 16 = 68.

The correct answer is not among the options provided, but based on the calculations, the number of different groups of presenters that can be chosen is {68}.
Final Answer: 68

--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine the maximum number of students who could have neither attended the prom night nor the debating session, we need to consider the minimum overlap between the two groups.

1. Calculate the number of students who attended the prom night:
- At least 45% attended the prom night.
- 45% of 200 students is 0.45 * 200 = 90 students.

2. Calculate the number of students who took part in the debating session:
- At least 35% took part in the debating session.
- 35% of 200 students is 0.35 * 200 = 70 students.

3. To find the maximum number of students who did neither, we assume the minimum overlap between the two groups. This means we assume that the students who attended the prom night and those who took part in the debating session are completely separate groups.

4. Add the number of students who attended the prom night and those who took part in the debating session:
- 90 (prom night) + 70 (debating session) = 160 students.

5. Subtract this total from the total number of students to find those who did neither:
- 200 students - 160 = 40 students.

- The correct calculation should be:
- Total students = 200
- Students who attended at least one event = 90 (prom night) + 70 (debating session) - overlap
- Maximum students who did neither = 200 - (90 + 70 - overlap)

Since the overlap cannot be negative, the maximum number of students who did neither is when the overlap is minimized, which is 0.

Therefore, the maximum number of students who could have neither attended the prom night nor the debating session is 200 - 90 - 70 = 40.

- If we assume the minimum overlap, the maximum number of students who did neither is 200 - 90 - 70 = 40, which is not an option.

We are told that one third of 3/4 of a number is 21.

Step 2: Set up the equation.

\(\frac{1}{3} \times \frac{3}{4} \times x = \frac{3}{12} \times x = \frac{1}{4} \times x\).

\(\frac{1}{4} \times x = 21\).

--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine how many minutes it will take for the cyclist to travel 48 miles, we need to use the given facts:

1. The cyclist's speed is 12 miles per hour.
2. The distance to be traveled is 48 miles.

First, we calculate the time in hours it takes to travel 48 miles at 12 miles per hour:

Time (in hours) = Distance / Speed = 48 miles / 12 miles per hour = 4 hours.

Next, we convert the time from hours to minutes. Since there are 60 minutes in an hour, we multiply the time in hours by 60:

Time (in minutes) = 4 hours * 60 minutes/hour = 240 minutes.

Therefore, it will take the cyclist 240 minutes to travel 48 miles. The answer is {B}.

--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
Last year, a Home Appliance Store sold an average(arithmetic mean) of 42 microwave ovens per month. In the first 10 months of this year, the store has sold an average(arithmetic mean) of only 20 microwave ovens per month. What was the average number of microwave ovens sold per month during the entire 22 months period? # Answer option: ['A)21', 'B)30', 'C)31', 'D)32', 'E)None of the above']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To find the average number of microwave ovens sold per month during the entire 22-month period, we need to calculate the total number of microwave ovens sold over these months and then divide by the total number of months.

Step 1: Calculate the total number of microwave ovens sold last year.
- Last year, the store sold an average of 42 microwave ovens per month.
- Assuming last year consists of 12 months, the total number sold last year is 42 ovens/month * 12 months = 504 ovens.

Step 2: Calculate the total number of microwave ovens sold in the first 10 months of this year.
- In the first 10 months of this year, the store sold an average of 20 microwave ovens per month.
- The total number sold in these 10 months is 20 ovens/month * 10 months = 200 ovens.

Step 3: Calculate the total number of microwave ovens sold over the entire 22-month period.
- Total ovens sold = 504 ovens (last year) + 200 ovens (first 10 months of this year) = 704 ovens.

Step 4: Calculate the average number of microwave ovens sold per month over the 22-month period.
- Total months = 12 months (last year) + 10 months (this year) = 22 months.
- Average = Total ovens sold / Total months = 704 ovens / 22 months = 32 ovens/month.

Therefore, the average number of microwave ovens sold per month during the entire 22-month period is {32}.
Final Answer: 32
Ground Truth Answer: d

### Reformatted Question:
In a bag of red and green sweets, the ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4. If the bag contains 120 green sweets, how many red sweets are there? # Answer option: ['A)90', 'B)80', 'C)95', 'D)100', 'E)85']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
In a bag of red and green sweets, the ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4. If the bag contains 120 green sweets, how many red sweets are there? # Answer option: ['A)90', 'B)80', 'C)95', 'D)100', 'E)85']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To find the number of red sweets, we need to use the given ratio and the number of green sweets.

1. We know the ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4. This means for every 3 red sweets, there are 4 green sweets.

2. We are given that the bag contains 120 green sweets.

3. To find the number of red sweets, we set up a proportion based on the ratio:
\[
\frac{\text{red sweets}}{\text{green sweets}} = \frac{3}{4}
\]

4. Let \( x \) be the number of red sweets. Then:
\[
\frac{x}{120} = \frac{3}{4}
\]

5. Solving for \( x \), we cross-multiply:
\[
4x = 3 \times 120
\]

6. Calculate the right side:
\[
3 \times 120 = 360
\]

7. Now solve for \( x \):
\[
4x = 360 \implies x = \frac{360}{4} = 90
\]

Therefore, there are 90 red sweets in the bag. The answer is {A)90}.
Final Answer: a)90

3. If each employee contributes Rs. 60 extra, as per , the new contribution per employee becomes \( \frac{600000}{n} + 60 \).

Question: A shopkeeper in order to promote his new shop put a discount of 20% on all the items for one day. Now he must sell the items at original price the other day. By what percentage must he increase the price to original? # Answer option: ['A)21%', 'B)20%', 'C)25%', 'D)33%', 'E)18%']
### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
The question involves a shopkeeper who initially offers a discount and then needs to return to the original price. The key facts needed to solve this problem are the percentage of the discount offered and the requirement to return to the original price. These facts are essential to determine the percentage increase needed to revert to the original price.

### Key Facts:
discount of 20%
must sell the items at original price

### Reformatted Question:
A shopkeeper in order to promote his new shop put a discount of 20% on all the items for one day. Now he must sell the items at original price the other day. By what percentage must he increase the price to original? # Answer option: ['A)21%', 'B)20%', 'C)25%', 'D)33%', 'E)18%']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
A shopkeeper in order to promote his new shop put a discount of 20% on all the items for one day. Now he must sell the items at original price the other day. By what percentage must he increase the price to original? # Answer option: ['A)21%', 'B)20%', 'C)25%', 'D)33%', 'E)18%']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine the percentage increase required to return the discounted price back to the original price.

1. Let's assume the original price of an item is $100.

2. The shopkeeper offers a discount of 20% on this price. Therefore, the discounted price is:
\[
100 - (20\% \text{ of } 100) = 100 - 20 = 80
\]

3. Now, the shopkeeper must sell the items at the original price the next day, which is $100.

4. To find the percentage increase needed to go from the discounted price ($80) back to the original price ($100), we use the formula for percentage increase:
\[
\text{Percentage Increase} = \left(\frac{\text{Original Price} - \text{Discounted Price}}{\text{Discounted Price}}\right) \times 100
\]
Substituting the values:
\[
\text{Percentage Increase} = \left(\frac{100 - 80}{80}\right) \times 100 = \left(\frac{20}{80}\right) \times 100 = 0.25 \times 100 = 25\%
\]

Therefore, the shopkeeper must increase the price by 25% to return to the original price. The correct answer is {C}.
Final Answer: c
Ground Truth Answer: c
Question: All 250 files on Sam's hard drive are infected by either a virus or a worm or both. The number of files that are infected only by a worm is 2.5 times the number of files that are infected by both a virus and a worm. If 50% of the files were not infected by a virus, how many of Sam's files were NOT infected by a worm? # Answer option: ['A)50', 'B)70', 'C)75', 'D)100', 'E)125']
### Fact Extraction Reasoning:
To determine how many of Sam's files were not infected by a worm, we need to focus on the relationships between the files infected by a virus, a worm, or both. The total number of files, the proportion not infected by a virus, and the relationship between files infected only by a worm and those infected by both are crucial to solving the problem.

### Key Facts:
All 250 files on Sam's hard drive are infected by either a virus or a worm or both
number of files that are infected only by a worm is 2.5 times the number of files that are infected by both a virus and a worm
50% of the files were not infected by a virus

### Reformatted Question:
All 250 files on Sam's hard drive are infected by either a virus or a worm or both. The number of files that are infected only by a worm is 2.5 times the number of files that are infected by both a virus and a worm. If 50% of the files were not infected by a virus, how many of Sam's files were NOT infected by a worm? # Answer option: ['A)50', 'B)70', 'C)75', 'D)100', 'E)125']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
All 250 files on Sam's hard drive are infected by either a virus or a worm or both. The number of files that are infected only by a worm is 2.5 times the number of files that are infected by both a virus and a worm. If 50% of the files were not infected by a virus, how many of Sam's files were NOT infected by a worm? # Answer option: ['A)50', 'B)70', 'C)75', 'D)100', 'E)125']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To solve this problem, we need to determine how many of Sam's files were not infected by a worm using the given facts.

1. **Total Files and Virus Infection**:
- According to , all 250 files are infected by either a virus, a worm, or both.
- states that 50% of the files were not infected by a virus. This means 50% of 250 files were not infected by a virus, which is 125 files.

2. **Files Infected by Worms**:
- Since 125 files are not infected by a virus, these files must be infected only by a worm because all files are infected by either a virus or a worm or both.

3. **Files Infected by Both**:
- Let the number of files infected by both a virus and a worm be \( x \).
- According to , the number of files infected only by a worm is 2.5 times the number of files infected by both. Therefore, the number of files infected only by a worm is \( 2.5x \).

4. **Equation Setup**:
- The total number of files infected by a worm (either only by a worm or by both) is the sum of files infected only by a worm and files infected by both, which is \( 2.5x + x = 3.5x \).
- We know from step 2 that 125 files are infected only by a worm, so \( 2.5x = 125 \).

5. **Solving for \( x \)**:
- Solve \( 2.5x = 125 \) to find \( x \).
- \( x = 125 / 2.5 = 50 \).

6. **Files Not Infected by a Worm**:
- The number of files infected by both a virus and a worm is \( x = 50 \).
- The total number of files infected by a worm is \( 3.5x = 3.5 \times 50 = 175 \).
- Therefore, the number of files not infected by a worm is the total number of files minus those infected by a worm: \( 250 - 175 = 75 \).

Thus, the number of Sam's files that were not infected by a worm is {C)75}.
Final Answer: c)75
Ground Truth Answer: c

In a class, 8% of total students are interested in Football. 4/5 of total students are interested in Cricket. 10% of total students are interested in Basketball and remaining 20 students are not interested in any games. --------------- End of Conversation ---------------
In a class, 8% of total students are interested in Football. 4/5 of total students are interested in Cricket. 10% of total students are interested in Basketball and remaining 20 students are not interested in any games. How many students are there in the class? # Answer option: ['A)850', 'B)800', 'C)900', 'D)950', 'E)1000']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To find the total number of students in the class, we need to account for all the students interested in different sports and those not interested in any games.

Let's denote the total number of students in the class as \( x \).

1. According to , 8% of the total students are interested in Football. This means \( 0.08x \) students are interested in Football.

2. According to , 4/5 of the total students are interested in Cricket. This means \( \frac{4}{5}x \) students are interested in Cricket.

3. According to , 10% of the total students are interested in Basketball. This means \( 0.10x \) students are interested in Basketball.

4. According to , the remaining 20 students are not interested in any games.

The sum of all these students should equal the total number of students in the class:

\[ 0.08x + \frac{4}{5}x + 0.10x + 20 = x \]

First, convert \(\frac{4}{5}\) to a decimal to make calculations easier:

\[ \frac{4}{5} = 0.80 \]

Now, substitute this into the equation:

\[ 0.08x + 0.80x + 0.10x + 20 = x \]

Combine the terms involving \( x \):

\[ 0.98x + 20 = x \]

Subtract \( 0.98x \) from both sides to isolate the constant:

\[ 20 = x - 0.98x \]

\[ 20 = 0.02x \]

Now, solve for \( x \) by dividing both sides by 0.02:

\[ x = \frac{20}{0.02} \]

\[ x = 1000 \]

Therefore, the total number of students in the class is 1000. The answer is {E}.
Final Answer: e
Ground Truth Answer: e

To find the actual selling price of the article before the discount, we need to understand that the price Vinit paid, Rs.4578, is after a 20% discount.

Let's denote the actual selling price as \( x \).

Given that there is a discount of 20%, Vinit paid 80% of the actual selling price.

So, we can set up the equation:

\[ 0.8x = \text{Rs.4578} \]

To find \( x \), we solve the equation:

\[ x = \frac{\text{Rs.4578}}{0.8} \]

Calculating this gives:

\[ x = \frac{4578}{0.8} = 5722.5 \]

Therefore, the actual selling price of the article is Rs.5723.

--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
The capacity of a tank of dimensions (8 m × 6 m × 2.5 m) is
# Answer option: ['A)120 litres', 'B)1200 litres', 'C)12000 litres', 'D)120000 litres', 'E)None of these']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine the capacity of the tank, we need to calculate its volume using the given dimensions.

Step 1: Calculate the volume of the tank.
The volume of a rectangular tank is calculated by multiplying its length, width, and height.

Given dimensions are:
8 m × 6 m × 2.5 m

Volume = 8 m × 6 m × 2.5 m

Step 2: Perform the multiplication.
Volume = 8 × 6 × 2.5 = 48 × 2.5 = 120 cubic meters

Step 3: Convert cubic meters to liters.
1 cubic meter is equivalent to 1,000 liters.

Therefore, 120 cubic meters = 120 × 1,000 liters = 120,000 liters

The capacity of the tank is 120,000 liters.

The correct answer is {D}.
Final Answer: d
Ground Truth Answer: d

### Reformatted Question:
If there are 5,000 voters out of which 20% are not eligible to vote and there are two candidates contesting. The winning candidate won by 15% of the votes. What is the total number of votes he got? # Answer option: ['A)3267', 'B)2678', 'C)2797', 'D)2300', 'E)2781']
--------------- End of Conversation ---------------
If there are 5,000 voters out of which 20% are not eligible to vote and there are two candidates contesting. The winning candidate won by 15% of the votes. What is the total number of votes he got? # Answer option: ['A)3267', 'B)2678', 'C)2797', 'D)2300', 'E)2781']
--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine the total number of votes the winning candidate received, we need to follow these steps:

1. **Calculate the number of eligible voters:**
- There are 5,000 voters in total.
- 20% are not eligible to vote.
- Therefore, the number of eligible voters is 80% of 5,000.
- Calculation: 5,000 * 0.80 = 4,000 eligible voters.

2. **Determine the number of votes the winning candidate received:**
- The winning candidate won by 15% of the votes.
- This means the winning candidate received 15% more votes than the other candidate.
- Let the number of votes the losing candidate received be \( x \).
- Then, the winning candidate received \( x + 0.15 \times 4,000 \) votes.
- Since the total number of votes is 4,000, we have:
\[
x + (x + 0.15 \times 4,000) = 4,000
\]
- Simplifying, we get:
\[
2x + 600 = 4,000
\]
- Solving for \( x \):
\[
2x = 4,000 - 600 = 3,400
\]
\[
x = 1,700
\]
- Therefore, the winning candidate received:
\[
1,700 + 0.15 \times 4,000 = 1,700 + 600 = 2,300
\]

Thus, the total number of votes the winning candidate got is {D)2300}.
Final Answer: d)2300
Ground Truth Answer: d
